add_namespace = csa
add_namespace = csa_sucsessor

### Constitution Events ###

###Social Patriots
country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - Property Debate
	id = csa.1000
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1000"}
	title = csa.1000.t
	desc = csa.1000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #The Laborists win out
		name = csa.1000.a	
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		set_variable = { CSA_afl = 1 }
		set_variable = { CSA_browder = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.1001
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # The Nationalists win out
		name = csa.1000.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		set_variable = { CSA_nationalists = 1 }
		set_variable = { CSA_burnham = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.1001
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - Social Radicalism
	id = csa.1001
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1001"}
	title = csa.1001.t
	desc = csa.1001.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	    option = { #The Laborists win out
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_SCOTT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOEB
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1001.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}	
		add_to_variable = { CSA_afl = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { CSA_burnham = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.1002
				days = 7
			}
		}
	    }
	    option = { # The Nationalists win out
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1001.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_to_variable = { CSA_nationalists = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { CSA_browder = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.1002
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - Voting Rights
	id = csa.1002
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1002"}
	title = csa.1002.t
	desc = csa.1002.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #The Laborite Plan
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war

					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOEB
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1002.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.08
		}
		country_event = {
			id = csa.1003
			days = 6
		}
		add_to_variable = { CSA_afl = 1 }
		set_country_flag = CSA_Laborite_Plan
	}
	option = { # The Nationalist Plan
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war

			}
		}

			ideology = radical_socialist

		}

			id = csa.1003
			days = 6
		}
		add_to_variable = { CSA_nationalists = 1 }
		set_country_flag = CSA_Nationalist_Plan
	}
	option = { # The Centralist Plan

			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_SCOTT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOEB
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war

					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1002.c

			ideology = totalist

		}

			id = csa.1003

country_event = { # Socialist Election Arrives
	id = csa.1003
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1003"}
	title = csa.1003.t
	desc = csa.1003.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #The Independence League
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_SCOTT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOEB
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_Centralist_Plan
				has_country_flag = CSA_Nationalist_Plan
				check_variable = { CSA_nationalists > 1 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.901
				days = 6
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.330
				days = 5
			}
			set_country_flag = CSA_Nationalist_Victory
			set_country_flag = CSA_syndicalism
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party_long
				name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				long_name = CSA_syndicalist_party_syndicalism_long
				name = CSA_syndicalist_syndicalism_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = CSA_radical_socialist_syndicalism_party_long
				name = CSA_radical_socialist_syndicalism_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = CSA_social_democrat_syndicalism_party_long
				name = CSA_social_democrat_syndicalism_party
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # The AFL
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_SCOTT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOEB
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_Laborite_Plan
				check_variable = { CSA_afl > 1 }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.901
				days = 6
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.325
				days = 5
			}
			set_country_flag = CSA_AFL_In_Power
			set_country_flag = CSA_syndicalism
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party_long
				name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				long_name = CSA_syndicalist_party_syndicalism_long
				name = CSA_syndicalist_syndicalism_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = CSA_radical_socialist_syndicalism_party_long
				name = CSA_radical_socialist_syndicalism_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = CSA_social_democrat_syndicalism_party_long
				name = CSA_social_democrat_syndicalism_party
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Browder's SPA Centralist Ticket
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_SCOTT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOEB
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { CSA_browder > 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.901
				days = 6
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BBR = {
						has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Harry Haywood"}
					}
				}
				BBR = {
					country_event = {
						id = bbr.28
						days = 35
					}
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = CSA_Ernest_Hemingway_for_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Gus_Hall_eco_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Steve_Nelson_sec_tot
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Earl Browder"
				desc = "POLITICS_EARL_BROWDER_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Earl_Browder_Hat.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = popcom_subtype
				traits = { CSA_new_founding_father }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.71
				days = 365
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.72
				days = 380
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.74
				days = 430
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name = CSA_totalist_browder_party_long
			name = CSA_totalist_browder_party 
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			long_name = CSA_syndicalist_federalist_party_long
			name = CSA_syndicalist_federalist_party
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			long_name = CSA_radical_socialist_federalist_party_long
			name = CSA_radical_socialist_federalist_party
		}
		country_event = {
			id = csa.50
			days = 7
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_Nationalists_in_power
		set_country_flag = CSA_party
	}
	option = { # The American Worker's Party
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.e
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { CSA_burnham > 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.901
				days = 6
			}
			set_country_flag = CSA_burnham_is_leader
			set_country_flag = CSA_party
			set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = CSA_Joseph_Zack_Kornfeder_for_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Frederick_L_Ackerman_eco_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Lawrence_Dennis_sec_tot 
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "James Burnham"
				desc = "POLITICS_JAMES_BURNHAM_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_James_Burnham.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = burnhamite_thought_subtype
				traits = { managerialist }
			}
			country_event = { id = csa.165 days = 8 }
			country_event = { id = csa.273 months = 2 }
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name = CSA_totalist_centralist_party_long
			name = CSA_totalist_centralist_party
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			long_name = CSA_syndicalist_federalist_party_long
			name = CSA_syndicalist_federalist_party
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			long_name = CSA_radical_socialist_federalist_party_long

country_event = { # Constitutional Convention begins
	id = csa.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1"}
	title = csa.1.t
	desc = csa.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "CSA Central Committee"
				desc = "POLITICS_CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = bellamyism_subtype
				traits = {
					our_right_to_survive
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "CSA Central Committee"
				desc = "POLITICS_CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = syndicalist_subtype
				traits = {
					our_right_to_survive
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "CSA Central Committee"
				desc = "POLITICS_CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authcom_subtype
				traits = {
					our_right_to_survive
				}
			}
			set_variable = { CSA_centralists = 0 }
			set_variable = { CSA_radicals = 0 }
			country_event = {
				id = csa.2
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - System of Government
	id = csa.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.2"}
	title = csa.2.t
	desc = csa.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		name = csa.2.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = CSA_radicals_gain_power
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CSA_syndicalism
			add_to_variable = { CSA_radicals = 1 }
			country_event = {
				id = csa.3
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FOSTER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BUTLER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_SYNDICALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.2.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = CSA_centralists_gain_power
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.10

			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			last_election = "1936.11.08"
			elections_allowed = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {

						has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Harry Haywood"}
					}
				}
				BBR = {
					country_event = {
						id = bbr.28
						days = 35
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Totalist - Capone
		name = csa.11.g
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { CSA_centralists > 1 }
			has_country_flag = CSA_smuggle
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FOSTER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BUTLER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_SYNDICALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_scarface
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alphonse Capone"
				desc = "POLITICS_CAPONE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Alphonse_Capone.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = caponism_subtype
				traits = { sec_prince_of_terror scarface }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
				election_frequency = 48
				last_election = "1936.11.08"
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			CSA_Jimmy_Hoffa_hog_tot
			CSA_Charles_Floyd_for_tot
			CSA_Bugsy_Siegel_eco_tot

country_event = { # 1940 Election
	id = csa.29
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.29 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = csa.29.t
	desc = csa.29.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1940_election
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		}
		date > 1940.1.1
		date < 1944.1.1
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.29.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1940_election
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.28
				days = 1230
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.2905
				days = 1237
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.290
				days = 1242
			}
			if = { limit = { has_government = social_democrat }
				country_event = {
					id = csa.3250
					days = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 IWW/SLP Primary
	id = csa.28
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.28 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = csa.28.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference1

	desc = { # IWW has the Presidency
		text = csa.28.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = syndicalist
		}
	}
	desc = { # IWW does not have the Presidency
		text = csa.28.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = syndicalist }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election
		}
		has_completed_focus = CSA_second_convention
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Eugene Dennis
		name = csa.28.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_1944_iww_primary_dennis
		set_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership
	}
	option = { # Arnold Petersen
		name = csa.28.b
		set_country_flag = CSA_1944_iww_primary_petersen
		set_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership
	}
	option = { # Elizabeth Nord
		name = csa.31.b
		set_country_flag = CSA_1944_iww_primary_nord
		set_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership
	}
	option = { # Louise Bryant
		name = csa.28.c
		set_country_flag = CSA_1944_iww_primary_bryant
		set_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership
	}
	option = { # Helen Keller
		name = csa.28.f
		set_country_flag = CSA_1944_iww_primary_keller
		set_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership
	}
	option = { # Sam Dolgoff
		name = csa.28.g
		set_country_flag = CSA_1944_iww_primary_dolgoff
		set_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership
	}
	option = { # Carlo Tresca
		name = csa.28.h
		set_country_flag = CSA_1944_iww_primary_tresca
		set_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership
	}
	option = { # Nominate the President
		name = csa.28.e
		trigger = {
			has_government = syndicalist
		}
	}
}

			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_ideas = {
			CSA_Asa_P_Randolph_for_rso
			CSA_John_L_Lewis_eco_rso
			CSA_Charles_Chaplin_sec_rso
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.39
				days = 5
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.31
				days = 1230
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.32
				days = 1237
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.322
				days = 1242
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Syndie
		name = csa.30.c
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1944_election_syndie
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_1940_election_ansynd
			}
			set_country_flag = CSA_1944_election_ansynd
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_1940_election_de_leonist
			}
			set_country_flag = CSA_1944_election_de_leonist
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_1940_election_orthodox
			}
			set_country_flag = CSA_1944_election_orthodox
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Ralph_Chaplin_for_syn
					CSA_Frank_Little_eco_syn
					CSA_Eugene_Dennis_sec_syn
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Carlo_Tresca_for_syn
					CSA_Wyndham_Mortimer_eco_syn
					CSA_Salaria_Kea_sec_syn
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Max_Shachtman_for_syn
					CSA_Harry_Bridges_eco_syn
					CSA_Lee_Pressman_sec_syn
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Smedley Butler " 
				}
			    }
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Max_Shachtman_for_syn
					CSA_Harry_Bridges_eco_syn

### 1948 Elections ###

country_event = { # 1948 IWW/SLP Primary
	id = csa.31
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.31"}
	title = csa.31.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	desc = { # IWW won the presidency just last time
		text = csa.31.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = syndicalist
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = csa_1944_election_syndie
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # IWW won also in 1940
		text = csa.31.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_country_flag = csa_1944_election_syndie
		}
	}
	desc = { # IWW does not have the Presidency
		text = csa.31.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Eric Hass
		name = csa.31.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CSA_1948_iww_primary_hass
			set_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership
				}
				clr_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership
				}
				clr_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Elizabeth Nord
		name = csa.31.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CSA_1948_iww_primary_nord
			set_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership
				}
				clr_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership
				}
				clr_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Sam Dolgoff
		name = csa.31.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CSA_1948_iww_primary_dolgoff
			set_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership
				}
				clr_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership
				}
				clr_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Nominate the President
		name = csa.31.e
		trigger = {
			has_government = syndicalist
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1948 Election
	id = csa.33

	desc = csa.33.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done

		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election

			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election

	immediate = {

				create_country_leader = {

				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Hugh Mulzac"
					desc = "POLITICS_MULZAC_DESC"

country_event = { # 1952 Election
	id = csa.36
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.36"}
	title = csa.36.t
	desc = csa.36.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Eugene Dennis
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_iww_primary_dennis }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Eugene Dennis"
					desc = "POLITICS_EUGENE_DENNIS_DESC"

						indecisive
					}

				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_iww_primary_blomen }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Henning A. Blomen"

					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Henning_A_Blomen.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = anarcho_syndicalist_subtype
					traits = {
						CSA_bloodless_revolutionary
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # John Bernard
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_iww_primary_bernard }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John Bernard"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_BERNARD_DESC"

					name = "Oakley C. Johnson"

					name = "Noam Chomsky"
					desc = "POLITICS_NOAM_CHOMSKY_DESC"

				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Daniel Hoan"

					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_democratic_socialism_subtype
					traits = {

					}

			}
			if = { # George Meany
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_afl_primary_meany }

				create_country_leader = {
					name = "George Meany"

				create_country_leader = {

	}
	
	option = { # SocDem
		name = csa.33.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1952_election_socdem
		}

			popularity = 0.05

			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_ideas = {
			CSA_Thomas_Kennedy_for_sde
			CSA_Reuben_Soderstrom_eco_sde
			CSA_Frank_J_Hayes_sec_sde
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.3703
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # IWW
		name = csa.36.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1952_election_iww
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Ralph_Chaplin_for_syn
					CSA_Frank_Little_eco_syn
					CSA_Eugene_Dennis_sec_syn
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Carlo_Tresca_for_syn
					CSA_Wyndham_Mortimer_eco_syn
					CSA_Salaria_Kea_sec_syn
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Max_Shachtman_for_syn
					CSA_Harry_Bridges_eco_syn
					CSA_Lee_Pressman_sec_syn
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.40
				days = 1
			}
			#no more primaries
		}
	}
	option = { # CIO
		name = csa.36.c
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1952_election_cio
			set_country_flag = CSA_Nationalist_Victory
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_ideas = {
			CSA_Asa_P_Randolph_for_rso
			CSA_John_L_Lewis_eco_rso
			CSA_Charles_Chaplin_sec_rso
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.40
				days = 1
			}
			#no more primaries
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The election(totalist)
	id = csa.51
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.51"}
	title = csa.51.t
	desc = csa.51.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		has_government = totalist
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = CSA_proletariat_commander }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_totalist_elections
			value = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = csa.51.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value > 0
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value < 2
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = csa.51.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value > 1
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value < 3
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = csa.51.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value > 2
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value < 4
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = csa.51.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value > 3
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Butler's Coup
	id = csa.67
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.67"}
	title = csa.67.t
	desc = csa.67.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = CSA_purge_reactionaries
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.67.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CSA_post_civil_war
					option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FOSTER
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.2
		add_political_power = -100
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.68
				days = 7
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_butlers_counter_coup
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		create_country_leader = {

country_event = { # The Atomic Chain Broken
	id = csa.128
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.128"}
	title = csa.128.t
	desc = csa.128.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # We hold the future now
		name = csa.128.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_tech = atomic_research }
				NOT = { is_researching_technology = atomic_research }
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = csa.128.t
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				technology = atomic_research
			}
			add_breakthrough_progress = {
				specialization = specialization_nuclear
				value = 0.25
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_breakthrough_progress = {
				specialization = specialization_nuclear
				value = 0.75
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Overtures to Mexico
	id = csa.130
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.130"}
	title = csa.130.t
	desc = csa.130.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.130.a #Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = USA_american_trade
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = ITA_likes_govt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					is_guaranteed_by = FROM
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				give_guarantee = MEX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					gives_military_access_to = FROM
				}
			}
			give_military_access = FROM
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_mainland_america = yes
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = MEX
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = MEX
				}
				remove_claim_by = MEX
			}
			CSA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = FROM
						is_claimed_by = FROM
					}
					is_mainland_america = no
					is_core_of = MEX
				}
				MEX = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.131
				hours = 8
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = csa.130.b #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_subject_of = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					has_opinion = {
						target = FROM
						value > 50
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = ITA_dislikes_govt
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.132
				hours = 8
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.191"}
	title = csa.191.t
	desc = csa.191.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Keep our name
		name = csa.191.a
	}
	option = { #United American Social Republic
		name = csa.191.b
			hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = CSA_burnham3_UASR
			}
	}
	option = { #Worker's Technocracy of America
		name = csa.191.c
			hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = CSA_burnham3_WTA
			}
	}

}

country_event = { # PCC
	id = csa.193
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.193"}
	title = csa.193.t
	desc = csa.193.d
	picture = GFX_CSA_iron_brigade2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Flavor
		name = csa.193.a
		if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1
					add_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1_PCC
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2
					add_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2_PCC
				}
			}
	}
	
	option = {
	name = csa.193.b
	}
}

country_event = { # Strengthen Iron Brigades
	id = csa.195
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.195"}
	title = csa.195.t
	desc = csa.195.d
	picture = GFX_event_CSA_iron_brigade

	trigger = {
	OR = {
		has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1_PCC
		has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2_PCC
		has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1
		has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2 }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { 
				name = csa.195.a
	
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1_PCC }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1_PCC
					add_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced_PCC
				}
				hidden_effect = {
				CSA = {
				country_event = {
				id = csa.196
				days = 50
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2_PCC }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2_PCC
					add_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced_PCC
				}
				hidden_effect = {
				CSA = {
				country_event = {
				id = csa.196
				days = 50
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1
					add_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced
				}
				hidden_effect = {
				CSA = {
				country_event = {
				id = csa.196
				days = 50
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2
					add_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced
				}
				hidden_effect = {
				CSA = {
				country_event = {
				id = csa.196
				days = 50
						}
					}
				}
			}
	}
	option = {				
	name = csa.195.b
	}

}

				}

				}
			}
	}

		}
	}

country_event = { # asking for New England Back
	id = csa.2700
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.2700"}
	title = csa.2700.t
	desc = csa.2700.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Lets not risk a war.
		name = csa.2700.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NEE = {
					exists = yes
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NEE = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				end_puppet = NEE
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
				NEE = {
					leave_faction = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NEE = {
						exists = yes
						has_war = yes
					}
				}
				NEE = {
					separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = CAN
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
					remove_claim_by = CAN
				}
				FROM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.2701
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # We shall never give into yankee arrogance
		name = csa.2700.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					has_war_with = GER
					has_war_with = FRA
					has_war_with = ENG
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				NEE = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.2702
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England has been returned to us
	id = csa.2701
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.2701"}
	title = csa.2701.t
	desc = csa.2701.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.2701.a
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = NEE }
			annex_country = {
				target = NEE
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = CAN
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}

country_event = { #Loeb
	id = csa.519030
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.51902" }
	title = csa.519030.t
	desc = csa.519030.d
		picture = event_CSA_Technocracy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Loeb Wins
		name = csa.519030.a
				set_cosmetic_tag = CSA_loeb_america
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			CSA_Ernest_Hemmingway_hog_rso
					CSA_Howard_Scott_for_tot
			CSA_Frederick_L_Ackerman_eco_tot
			CSA_Dal_Hitchcock_sec_tot
		}
				set_party_name = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						name = CSA_utopian_technocrat_party
						long_name = CSA_utopian_technocrat_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
						ideology = social_democrat
						name = CSA_utopian_technocrat_party
						long_name = CSA_utopian_technocrat_party_long
				}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Harold Loeb"
			desc = ""
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Harold_Loeb.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = socdem_utopian_technocracy_subtype
			traits = { CSA_utopian_technocrat_traits }
				}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Harold Loeb"
			desc = ""
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Harold_Loeb.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = utopian_technocracy_subtype
			traits = { CSA_utopian_technocrat_traits }
		}
		 }
			set_politics = {
			   ruling_party = radical_socialist
			   elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_socdem_to_coalition = yes
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				current_tot_pop = party_popularity@totalist
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_radsoc_pop = party_popularity@radical_socialist
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_tot_pop
				value = current_radsoc_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = current_tot_pop
			}
			remove_ideas = CSA_emergency_powers_idea
			remove_ideas = CSA_proletariat_duties_idea
			remove_ideas = CSA_proletariat_duties_idea2
			remove_ideas = CSA_continental_socialist_society_idea
			remove_ideas = CSA_proletariat_commander_idea
			remove_ideas = CSA_proletariat_commander_idea_2
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_3
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1_PCC
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_2_PCC
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced_PCC
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced_PCC_weapons
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced_weapons
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced_rigged
			remove_ideas = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced_PCC_rigged
			remove_ideas = CSA_continental_constabularly_idea
			remove_ideas = CSA_energy_accounting_idea
			remove_ideas = CSA_energy_accounting_idea_2
			remove_ideas = CSA_four_hour_work_week
			remove_ideas = CSA_female_auxilaries_idea
			remove_ideas = CSA_social_units_idea
			remove_ideas = CSA_technocratic_empire_idea
			remove_ideas = CSA_biological_weapons
			remove_ideas = CSA_napalm_idea
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				name = CSA_technocracy_inc_party
				long_name = CSA_technocracy_inc_party_long
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Howard Scott"
				desc = "POLITICS_HOWARD_SCOTT_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Howard_Scott.png"

		name = csa.6011.b
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_2 = yes
		add_political_power = 25
	}
	option = { #nah
	    trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_ideology = burnhamite_thought_subtype
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = CSA_la_cosa_nostra
                    NOT = {
						has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Clyde Barrow" }
					    has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "René Belbenoît" }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.6011.c	
		add_stability = 0.02
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # Take a Vacation?
	id = csa_sucsessor.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa_sucsessor.1"}
	title = csa_sucsessor.1.t
	desc = csa_sucsessor.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #yes
		name = csa_sucsessor.1.a	
		
	}

	option = { #no
		name = csa_sucsessor.1.b	
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Earl Browder"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = csa_sucsessor.3
					days = 33
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "William Z. Foster"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = csa_sucsessor.4
					days = 33
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "James Burnham"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = csa_sucsessor.2
					days = 33
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
